\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2liblodepng_2lodepng_8cpp_source_l00438}00438 \textcolor{comment}{  a good huffman tree has N * 2 -\/ 1 nodes, of which N -\/ 1 are internal nodes. Here, the internal nodes are stored (what their 0 and 1 option point to). There is only memory for such good tree currently, if there are more nodes (due to too long length codes), error 55 will happen*/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2liblodepng_2lodepng_8cpp_source_l02033}02033 \textcolor{comment}{  For PNG filter method 0}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2liblodepng_2lodepng_8cpp_source_l02034}02034 \textcolor{comment}{  out must be a buffer with as size: h + (w * h * bpp + 7) / 8, because there are the scanlines with 1 extra byte per scanline}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2liblodepng_2lodepng_8cpp_source_l02035}02035 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2liblodepng_2lodepng_8cpp_source_l02036}02036 \textcolor{comment}{  There is a nice heuristic described here: http://www.cs.toronto.edu/\string~cosmin/pngtech/optipng.html. It says:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2liblodepng_2lodepng_8cpp_source_l02037}02037 \textcolor{comment}{   *  If the image type is Palette, or the bit depth is smaller than 8, then do not filter the image (i.e. use fixed filtering, with the filter None).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2liblodepng_2lodepng_8cpp_source_l02038}02038 \textcolor{comment}{   * (The other case) If the image type is Grayscale or RGB (with or without Alpha), and the bit depth is not smaller than 8, then use adaptive filtering heuristic as follows: independently for each row, apply all five filters and select the filter that produces the smallest sum of absolute values per row.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2liblodepng_2lodepng_8cpp_source_l02039}02039 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2liblodepng_2lodepng_8cpp_source_l02040}02040 \textcolor{comment}{  Here the above method is used mostly. Note though that it appears to be better to use the adaptive filtering on the plasma 8-\/bit palette example, but that image isn't the best reference for palette images in general.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\Hypertarget{build_2doxygen_2liblodepng_2lodepng_8cpp_source_l02041}02041 \textcolor{comment}{  */}}
